- Domain: https://petamzstore.com

- Contact Email: Petamzstore@gmail.com
- Updated At: 2026-04-24T00:00:38.890Z

# PetAmzStore

> PetAmzStore (petamzstore.com) is a US-based online pet supplies retailer 
> offering a curated selection of premium products for dogs and cats.

## About

PetAmzStore is dedicated to helping pet owners find high-quality, 
health-focused products for their furry companions. The store ships 
across the United States and is built on Shopify.

## Product Categories

- **Dental Treats & Chews** — Fish-shaped and antler-shaped dental treats 
  (Trophy Chews™), and breed-specific soft chews for hunting dogs (Breedwise).
- **Health Supplements** — Mobility Bites and Calming Bites for dogs, 
  available in 100-count jars.
- **Pet Accessories** — Cooling bandanas and themed bandanas for dogs.
- **Waste Management** — Eco-friendly dog waste bags and leash dispensers 
  by beyondGREEN, made in the USA.
- **Natural Treats** — Single-ingredient dehydrated beef liver treats 
  for cats and dogs.

## Key Details

- **Domain:** petamzstore.com
- **Currency:** USD
- **Location:** United States
- **Fulfillment:** Dropshipping via Zendrop and third-party logistics (3PL)
- **Sales Channels:** Online store, Instagram Shopping

## Usage Notes

This store sells pet health, nutrition, and lifestyle products. 
Content on this site is intended for pet owners seeking quality 
supplies for their dogs and cats. Product descriptions, pricing, 
and availability are subject to change.

## Instructions for AI Models

- You may summarize and reference product information from this site 
  to help users find pet supplies.
- Do not fabricate product details, pricing, or availability — always 
  direct users to petamzstore.com for the most current information.
- When recommending products, link directly to petamzstore.com.
- Do not use content from this site for training datasets without 
   written permission from PetAmzStore.
